--
-- Table structure for table `cashier`
--

CREATE TABLE `cashier` (
  `cashier_id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `partner_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `is_loggedin` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `loggin_time` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `is_locked` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `is_active` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `login_attempts` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `speed_range` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 3,
  `sound` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  `cashier_package` varchar(256) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `category` varchar(256) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'default',
  `cashier_profit` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `is_online` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `last_heartbeat` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp(),
  `cashier_bonus_status` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `cashier_fixed_bonus_amount` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 100,
  `color` varchar(256) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'three',
  `min_bet_birr` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 10,
  `last_updated` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp(),
  `winner_card` longtext DEFAULT NULL,
  `new_bonus_status` varchar(256) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'off',
  `auto_check_result` varchar(256) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'manual',
  `max_new_bonus_per_day` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  `good_bingo_sound` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `last` longtext DEFAULT NULL,
  `mid` varchar(256) DEFAULT NULL,
  `settings_json` longtext NOT NULL DEFAULT '{"bonus":{"status":"on","amount":"50","per_day":"1"},"system":{"check_result":"manual","color_mode":"three","profit":"0","good_bingo_sound":"0"},"toggles":{"will_start":true,"started":true,"stopped":true,"show_card_count":true}}',
  `profit_json` longtext NOT NULL DEFAULT '\r\n{\r\n  "commission_tiers": [\r\n    {"min": 3, "max": 5, "percent": 16},\r\n    {"min": 6, "max": 10, "percent": 17},\r\n    {"min": 11, "max": 20, "percent": 20},\r\n    {"min": 21, "max": 30, "percent": 25},\r\n    {"min": 31, "max": 40, "percent": 28},\r\n    {"min": 41, "max": 50, "percent": 30},\r\n    {"min": 51, "max": 60, "percent": 32},\r\n    {"min": 61, "max": 1000, "percent": 35}\r\n  ]\r\n}' COMMENT 'Bingo profit commission structure'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COLLATE=latin1_swedish_ci;

  `bonus_eligiblity_starts_from` varchar(256) NOT NULL DEFAULT '100',
  `edit_partner_permission` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  `lock_round_up_last_digit` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COLLATE=latin1_swedish_ci;

--
-- Table structure for table `transaction`
--

CREATE TABLE `transaction` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `cashier_id` varchar(256) NOT NULL,
  `game_round` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `santim` varchar(256) NOT NULL,
  `sew` varchar(256) NOT NULL,
  `income` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `bonus` decimal(10,0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `date` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
  `result` longtext DEFAULT NULL,
  `checked_number` varchar(256) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

--
-- Table structure for table `transaction_logs`
--

CREATE TABLE `transaction_logs` (
  `transaction_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `event_type` enum('transaction') NOT NULL,
  `timestamp` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
  `done_by` varchar(256) NOT NULL,
  `role` enum('Admin','Agent') NOT NULL,
  `action` enum('deposit_to_cashier','withdraw_from_cashier','deposit_to_partner','withdraw_from_partner') NOT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `cashier_id` varchar(256) DEFAULT NULL,
  `partner_id` varchar(256) DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('success','failure') NOT NULL,
  `message` text NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COLLATE=latin1_swedish_ci;

-- Dumping data for table `transaction_logs`
